--- [What's the readout in rolling shutter for APS-C crop vs full frame? : r/sigmafp] ---
What's the readout in rolling shutter for APS-C crop vs full frame? I have seen people saying APS-C has better readout time but can't find the exact number. IN IMAGE INFORMATION VIEW: Rotate the Rear Dial to display the previous or next images. ... HISTOGRAM The histogram is a graphic representation of the distribution of brightness in a picture. The horizontal axis shows the tone values from black (left) through gray to white (right). The vertical axis corresponds to the number of pixels at each brightness level.
